### [139] [Canonical separating coordinates in the generalized cubic Hénon-Heiles systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19188)
*Alessandro Portaluri,Nicola Sottocornola*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: Error


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Error

Method: Error

Result: Error

Conclusion: Error

Abstract: We study the three classical integrable generalized cubic Hénon--Heiles systems -- Kaup--Kupershmidt, KdV$_5$, and Sawada--Kotera -- from the viewpoint of bi-Hamiltonian geometry and separation of variables. On the standard symplectic manifold $T^*\mathbb R^2$, we construct compatible Poisson deformations $P_1=L_XP_0$, compute the associated recursion operators $N=P_1P_0^{-1}$, and analyze the action of $N^*$ on the codistribution generated by the first integrals. This yields the corresponding control matrices, whose eigenvalues provide the separating coordinates.
  For the generalized Kaup--Kupershmidt case we carry out the construction explicitly: we determine a deformation vector field, the compatible Poisson tensor, the torsionless recursion operator, the control matrix, the separating coordinates, and, crucially, the conjugate momenta. We then derive the separated relations and write the Hamilton equations in canonical separated variables, thus decomposing the original Hamiltonian system into two separated subsystems. To the best of our knowledge, this explicit derivation of the separating variables and, in particular, of the conjugate momenta for the generalized Kaup--Kupershmidt system is new.
  For the KdV$_5$ and Sawada--Kotera cases we show how the same bi-Hamiltonian scheme applies, emphasizing both the common geometric mechanism and the features peculiar to each system. In this way, the three generalized cubic Hénon--Heiles systems are treated within a unified framework based on compatible Poisson structures, recursion operators, control matrices, and Darboux--Nijenhuis coordinates.

*Kell Fremouw,Ryan A. DeCrescent,Xianfu Zhang,Yi Yang,Bin Chen,Daniel A. Morales,Matteo R. S. Poma,Kelly Schutt,Fangyuan Jiang,Edward H. Sargent,Neal R. Armstrong,David S. Ginger,Joseph M. Luther,Michael D. McGehee*

Abstract: Gradual reverse-bias breakdown in metal-halide perovskite diodes and solar cells is thought to originate from hole tunneling through steep bands in an ionic depletion region near the electron transport layer after positively charged iodine vacancies accumulate near the hole-transport layer (HTL). However, typical reported mobile ion concentrations near $1\times10^{17}$ cm$^{-3}$ are too small to quantitatively explain significant tunneling current densities and (Zener) breakdown observed near $-5$ V. Here, we show that inferred mobile ion concentrations increase by more than 100$\times$, to over $1\times10^{18}$ cm$^{-3}$, within just three minutes of reverse bias at $-6.0$ V in p-i-n perovskite diodes. We attribute the increase in mobile ion concentration to iodide oxidation and the resulting iodine vacancy creation which must be balanced by reduction reactions near the HTL. Thin and sub-optimal HTL coverage leads to direct contact between the transparent conducting electrode and perovskite and facilitates electron transfer and reduction, enabling the creation of even larger inferred mobile ion concentrations ($\sim1\times10^{19}$ cm$^{-3}$) and leading to faster degradation under reverse bias. This explains previous work that showed increased breakdown voltages and improved reverse-bias stability by implementing thick, uniform HTLs.

### [143] [Competition between acoustic radiation force and streaming-induced drag force in focused beams for 3D cell trapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19050)
*Shiyu Li,Zhixiong Gong*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 这项研究探讨了三度空间中利用声波捕获单细胞或多微粒的方法，提出了一个综合性的理论和数值模型来分析声辐射力和流体动力学阻尼力的相互作用。他们发现，在粘性流限和惯性流限中， streaming速度与焦点压力幅度的标量指数分别为 2 和 4/3，在过渡流限流动中则介于两者之间。通过对 Schiller-Naumann 模型的分析校正了阻尼力的估计，发现声辐射力与阻尼力的比值随焦点压力幅度变化呈现非线性关系，而非预期中的单调增加。这项研究为优化单束声波 tweezers 的三维捕获提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Optical tweezers 在生物医学和微流控领域有广泛应用，而声波作为一种更环保、更高效的手段，其三维捕获能力备受关注。然而，3D 捕获在高频条件下面临挑战，尤其是推力导致的阻尼效应尚未被系统性研究。因此，深入理解并优化声波捕获过程对于提升捕获效率至关重要。

Method: 该研究通过建立通用的理论框架和数值模拟，整合声辐射力和流体动力学模型。首先，推导了 streaming 速度的通用标量指数关系，在不同流态下分别得到 n=2、n=4/3 和介于两者之间的结果。其次，引入 Schiller-Naumann 模型校正了阻尼力的估计。最后，通过分析比值随焦点压力幅度的变化，揭示了其非线性行为。

Result: 研究发现了 streaming 速度与焦点压力幅度的关系在不同流态下的指数值，并提供了一个综合模型来比较声辐射力和阻尼力。通过引入更精确的阻尼模型，发现声辐射力与阻尼力的比值随焦点压力幅度变化呈非线性关系。这为优化声波 twez 耳件提供了理论依据，特别是其对 3D 捕获的稳定性优化具有重要意义。

Conclusion: 这项研究为声波三维捕获技术的发展提供了关键性的理论支持。通过对流态的全面分析，揭示了声辐射力与流体动力学阻尼力的复杂关系。结果对优化单束声波 tweezers 的设计和应用具有重要的指导意义，特别是对提高捕获效率和稳定性有所帮助。未来的工作可以扩展到多束声波或复合介质环境，以进一步提升捕获能力。

Abstract: The ability to trap a single cell or microparticle in three dimensions is important for biomedical and microfluidic applications. Single-beam acoustic tweezers based on focused waves provide a compact and biocompatible approach because of their high spatial resolution and strong intensity gradients. However, 3D trapping remains challenging, especially at high frequencies, because the weak axial restoring radiation force may not overcome the pushing drag force caused by acoustic bulk streaming in free space. The combined effect of acoustic radiation force and streaming-induced drag force on a microparticle has not been systematically studied. Although the radiation force scales with the square of the focal pressure amplitude p_foc, the scaling of streaming-induced drag force with p_foc under different flow conditions remains unclear. Here, we establish a unified theoretical and numerical framework to compare these two effects and derive an explicit scaling law, U0 ~ p_foc^n, for the streaming velocity from the viscous to the inertial regime. We show that n = 2 in the viscous limit (Re_lambda << 1), n = 4/3 in the inertial limit (Re_lambda >> 1), and n lies between 4/3 and 2 in the transition regime (Re_lambda ~ 1). We further introduce the Schiller-Naumann model to estimate the drag force more accurately than the Stokes model. On this basis, we find that the ratio of axial radiation force to drag can vary non-monotonically with p_foc, contrary to the conventional expectation of monotonic increase. This work provides a theoretical basis for optimizing single-beam acoustic tweezers for stable 3D trapping of single cells.

### [144] [Articulatory movements influence electromagnetic wave transmission through the vocal tract](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19362)
*Remi Blandin,Martin Laabs,Rudolf von Bunau,Bryn Lloyd,Silvia Farcito,Denys Nikolayev,Gabriela Hossu,Peter Birkholz,Dirk Plettemeier*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验验证了一种电磁波在人类头中美发音过程的数值模型，目的是更好地理解这一物理现象。研究人员使用磁共振成像创建了一个真实的有限元模型，并将其与测量数据进行比较，发现模型和测量数据在一定程度上一致，证明了该方法的有效性。研究结果表明，对相同的元音来说，不同说话者的传输系数模式相似。在研究的频率范围内，电场呈现出Mie散射模式。传入系数的形状由共振模式和 antenna 安装方式的综合作用决定，而开口的大小影响了散射模式的形状。尽管技术上具有挑战性，但这种数值方法对于研究人类头中的电磁波传播是非常有效的。该研究结果将有助于开发基于射频的静默语音接口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究人员使用磁共振成像对三个元音（/a/, /i/, 和 /u/)  singers 的头部进行扫描，创建了一个现实的有限元模型。随后，该模型与通过两个 subject 的散射矩阵测量数据进行了校准。研究过程中，尽管存在一些潜在的不一致来源，但模拟和测量数据在一定程度上一致。研究人员还观察到，相同的元音在不同的 subject 中的传输系数模式相似。此外，研究还发现，在研究的频率范围内（1-6 GHz），电场呈现 Mie 散射模式。此外，通过分析局部极小值和极大值（对应不同的语言发音 Configuration），研究人员发现这些变化与局部电场幅度的变化有关。传输系数的形状是不同共振模式和 antenna 置息的综合作用的结果。此外，研究人员还发现，开口大小影响散射模式的形状。

Result: 研究结果表明，该数值模型有效验证了电磁波在人类头中美发音过程的行为。具体来说，研究结果包括：1. 研究者模拟并测量了相同元音在不同 subject 中的传输系数，发现它们的模式相似。2. 在 1-6 GHz 的频率范围内，电场呈现出 Mie 散射模式。3. 通过分析局部极小和极大值，研究人员发现它们对应不同发音 Configuration，与局部电场幅度的变化相关。4. 传输系数的形状是不同共振模式和 antenna 安装方式的综合作用结果。5. 开口大小影响了散射模式的形状。尽管存在一些潜在的不一致性来源，但研究结果证明该方法在理论上是有效的，为开发基于射频的静默语音接口提供了理论依据。

Conclusion: 该研究通过实验验证了电磁波在人类头中美发音过程的数值模型，为深入理解这一物理现象提供了新的方法和工具。研究结果表明，该方法在理论上是可以有效应用于研究头部内的电磁波传播的。研究结果还表明，该方法可以为开发基于射频的静默语音接口提供重要的理论依据。总体而言，该研究在理论上和应用上都具有重要意义。

Abstract: This study experimentally validates a numerical model of electromagnetic propagation through the human head during the pronunciation of different vowels, with the goal of improving our understanding of the underlying physical phenomena. A realistic finite element model was created from magnetic resonance images acquired while pronouncing the vowels /a/, /i/, and /u/. The model was validated against scattering matrix measurements obtained from two subjects whose geometries were modeled. Despite several potential sources of discrepancy, the simulations and measurements showed good qualitative agreement, confirming the validity of the approach. Similar transmission coefficient patterns were observed across subjects for the same vowels. Within the investigated frequency range of (1-6 GHz), the electric field exhibited a Mie scattering pattern. Local minima and maxima in the transmission coefficient, characterizing different articulatory configurations, were correlated with local variations in the electric field amplitude. The transmission coefficient's shape results from an interplay between resonance patterns and antenna placement, while the degree of mouth opening influences the shape of scattering modes. Although technically challenging, this numerical approach proved effective for studying electromagnetic propagation in the human head. The resulting robust numerical model and improved understanding of the underlying physics are expected to facilitate the development of radio-frequency-based silent speech interfaces.

### [145] [Low noise resonant amplification by optical injection-locking and residual phase noise cancellation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18772)

Motivation: Error

Method: Error

Abstract: We demonstrate a low noise, high-gain, resonant optical amplifier that combines injection locking with feed-forward cancellation of residual phase noise. The wavelength-agnostic architecture uses a commercial semiconductor diode laser as a power amplifier while preserving the spectral purity of a weak reference. Although injection locking enforces phase coherence, finite residual phase noise within the locking regime limits high-fidelity transfer of low phase noise from the reference laser to the injection-locked laser, particularly at large gain. Here, the residual phase error is measured via optical heterodyne detection and canceled using feed-forward phase correction. Compared to injection locking alone, the amplifier achieves up to 38 dB phase-noise reduction at Fourier frequencies above 1 kHz for injection ratios down to -57 dB. This approach enables ASE-free amplification of low-power, low-noise optical references, including individual lines from optical frequency combs.

### [146] [Multi-slit time-reversed Young interference: source-space grating laws, quadratic-phase effects, and Talbot-like revivals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19524)
*Jianming Wen*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: We expand the time-reversed Young interferometer to multi-slit configurations and reveal new physics including quadratic Fresnel phases and Talbot revivals in source space.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding interference patterns in extended geometries is fundamental for optics and quantum mechanics.

Method: Mathematical analysis of interference in various slit configurations.

Result: Multi-slit systems exhibit quadratic phase effects and Talbot revivals, extending beyond two-slit phenomena.

Conclusion: Multi-slit time-reversed interferometers offer richer physics for applications like imaging and sensing.

Abstract: We develop a compact theory of time-reversed Young (TRY) interference beyond the symmetric two-slit geometry by considering equally spaced three-slit, finite $N$-slit, and infinite periodic slit arrays. In the TRY configuration, a point emitter illuminates the aperture, a position-fixed detector records the signal, and the response is reconstructed in source space by correlating the detector record with the source-coordinate label. We show that the three-slit case already reveals the essential new physics beyond two slits: a quadratic Fresnel phase survives, modifies the reconstructed interference law, and lifts the nominal dark fringes in the generic case. For a general equally spaced $N$-slit array, we identify the exact reconstructed response and show that the familiar textbook grating factor is recovered only when the quadratic phase is negligible, compensated, or reduced to a common phase across the array. In that ideal limit, the reconstructed peaks are source-space analogues of classical grating orders rather than outgoing diffraction beams. For an infinite periodic TRY array, we further show that the same discrete quadratic phase generates full and fractional Talbot-like revivals in source space, governed by a reciprocal-distance condition rather than the conventional Talbot propagation law. These results show that the symmetric two-slit TRY geometry is exceptional, while multi-slit TRY systems naturally combine source-space discrimination with sensitivity to aperture-wide phase structure and periodic-array revival physics.

Abstract: Metasurfaces have emerged as a powerful platform for compact optical sensors by replacing bulky lenses with flat arrays of subwavelength nanostructures. In precision optical metrology, the simultaneous mapping of a beam's polarization state and wavefront is crucial for real-time diagnostics of stress-induced birefringence and surface flatness. To achieve this in a compact footprint, existing metasurfaces typically partition their aperture into discrete zones, which inherently restricts the light-gathering efficiency and numerical aperture of the system. Here we demonstrate an inverse-designed metasurface that integrates full-Stokes polarimetry and Shack-Hartmann wavefront sensing within a single, continuous aperture in the visible spectrum. By leveraging an adjoint optimization approach to independently control the geometry and rotation of each nanostructure, we break the aperture-sharing paradigm and utilize the entire pixel area for all channels. When coupled with a shallow neural network to automate peak identification and correct for hardware non-idealities, our device yields a mean polarization reconstruction error of only 0.046 across 100 test states on the Poincaré sphere, while simultaneously maintaining the precise focal-spot tracking required for sensitive wavefront tilt detection. This work highlights the capacity of inverse design to generate multifunctional, non-intuitive flat optics that outperforms its traditional counterparts.

### [149] [Fast projections of two-dimensional light patterns using acousto-optical deflectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19421)
*Robbert Decruyenaere,Clara Tanghe,Senne Van Wellen,Karel Van Acoleyen*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: Error


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Error

Method: Error

Result: Error

Conclusion: Error

Abstract: Precise and flexible control of structured light fields is essential for applications ranging from optical trapping and quantum simulation to microscopy and materials processing. Acousto-optical deflectors (AODs) are widely used in these settings due to their high speed, large damage threshold, and ability to generate steerable optical tweezers. Multi-tone driving offers a powerful alternative to slow sequential scanning, enabling the projection of complex patterns with high accuracy as rapid acoustic modulation averages out inter-spot interference. In two dimensions, however, intermodulation between tones in orthogonal AODs can reintroduce coherent artifacts. We present a fast, feedback-free AOD projection scheme based on an incommensurately staggered frequency lattice that intrinsically suppresses such artifacts. For separable two-dimensional target patterns, our method removes the need for scanning entirely, enabling substantially faster and highly accurate projections. We further extend the approach to non-separable images using a minimal scanning strategy that maintains rather high projection speeds. These results demonstrate that appropriately engineered multi-tone AOD driving offers an efficient and robust route to high-speed, high-fidelity generation of arbitrary intensity patterns.

### [150] [Petabit-per-second Random Number Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18971)
*Lin Jiang,Jihui Sun,Qiao Zhang,Jincheng Cui,Xiaohan Wang,Yanlan Xiao,Lin Sun,Hairong Lin,Haijun He,Jiacheng Feng,Anlin Yi,Jia Ye,Xihua Zou,Wei Pan,Gangxiang Shen,Heng Zhou,Lianshan Yan*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于时钟微分波片的随机数生成系统，通过复杂非线性动力学和多信道并行技术，实现了单信道信源的宽频和低相关性，最终构建了每秒10.32 petabit的并行随机数生成系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着现代通信和计算对随机数生成的需求不断增加，特别是高吞吐量和并行处理的要求，开发高效的物理随机数生成器变得至关重要。微分波片在该领域的应用日益广泛，如何利用其复杂的非线性动力学特性来实现高效的随机数生成成为了研究者的关注焦点。

Method: 论文提出了一种基于时钟微分波片的系统，通过调制方式实现了单信道信源的有效带宽从440MHz提升至27.6GHz。进一步地，利用瑞利散射引入随机相位变化，从而降低了平行信道间的高度相关性，实现了高质量的随机数。系统还通过多通道检测技术，优化了信道间的相关性，最终达到了单通道14.336 Tbit/s和整体1.032 Pbit/s的总数据率。

Result: 论文最终实现了单个微分波片和光纤散射系统的全息可扩展性。设计的系统在不在线处理流程下，单通道的比特率达到了14.336 Tbit/s，总比特率则超过1.032 Pbit/s。这一成果是当前单通道以及整个系统领域的最高报告。系统能够通过扩展微分波片的可用信道或增加光纤散射链路的数量来显著提高吞吐量，为高渠道数和高速率的随机数生成奠定了基础。

Conclusion: 该论文通过创新性的方法和技术，为物理随机数生成器的应用提供了一个高效、可靠和可扩展的解决方案。利用微分波片的复杂动态特性和多信道平行处理，该系统不仅在单通道处理上表现优异，而且在多通道并行处理方面也有着显著的优势， paving了高吞吐量随机数生成的实际应用之路。

Abstract: Physical random number generators based on chaotic microcombs, with their complex nonlinear dynamics and multi-channel parallel capability, have attracted considerable research attention. However, key technical challenges for chaotic microcombs are the high correlation between symmetric teeth and the low bandwidth of single-channel teeth, which seriously affect the speed and scalability of random number generation. We experimentally demonstrate a petabit-per-second (Pbit/s) parallel random number generation system based on intensity chaotic modulation and Rayleigh scattering. Through intensity modulation, the effective bandwidth of the single-channel entropy source is increased from 440MHz to 27.6GHz. Crucially, Rayleigh scattering further contributes through the random superposition of backscattered light, which introduces unpredictable fluctuations in intensity, phase, and polarization. This randomness suppresses inter-channel correlation among parallel entropy sources to ~0.02, ensuring their orthogonality. Moreover, by employing polarization-diverse coherent detection on a single-channel, four new low correlated sub-channels are extracted: X-/Y- intensity and phase. We achieve a single-channel bit rate of 14.336 Tbit/s and a total bit rate of 1.032 Pbit/s (over 72 parallel channels) with offline post-processing, representing the highest post-processing record reported in both the single-channel and the total system. Moreover, our scheme based on a single chaotic microcomb and fiber scattering link show fundamentally scalable. The total bit rate can be significantly pushed beyond the Pbit/s level by further expanding the usable comb channel and/or by deploying multiple fiber scattering links in parallel, paving a practical path toward higher throughput regimes.

</details>


### [151] [Integrated Supermode Photonics Enabled by Supersymmetric Transformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18999)
*Kaile Chen,Qi Lu,Yuan Zhong,Jingchi Li,Yuru Li,Zhaohui Li,Chao Lu,Yikai Su,Lu Sun*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: ) 本研究提出了一种系统化方法来获得等间距有效索引分布的超模式，并能够通过高精度激发任意目标超模式。通过多阱光学势的实现方法（经过精心设计的波导阵列），支持的超模式具有最大的间距，并且可以实现等间距的效率索引分布。特别地，我们开发了一种二阶离散超对称( DSUSY )变换方法，这种方法能够同时激发和检测两个超模式，而且可以通过简单的级联结构扩展到任意数量的超模式。综上所述，我们的研究解决了分立超模式光子学中的长期瓶颈问题，并为使用超模式作为新的编码、传输和处理信息自由度提供了可扩展的方法。我们通过实现两个和四个超模式多复用系统，实验验证了这种方法的可行性和普适性。据我们所知，在所有模式通道上，这种设计的器件在100nm波长范围内（1500-1600纳米）具有较低的插入损失（<2.48dB @1550nm）和较低的信道间干扰（<-18dB @1550nm）。在四通道系统中进行的高速光通信实验，实现了1.024Tb/s的数据传输速率并保持了显著低的比特错误率。这些结果证明了超模式光子学的高容量和集成光学通信潜力。该研究奠定了集成分立超模式光子学的基础，将超模式作为光操作的新自由度，并为基于超模式的应用开辟了新的前景，包括但不限于集成光子通信、智能光计算和量子信息技术。 


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光通信技术的快速发展推动了集成光子学的发展，而超模式的引入为光子学提供了一个新的自由度，从而可能实现高容量集成光通信。为了实现超模式的有效度最大化和高精度激发，研究者需要一种系统化的方法来控制和激发超模式。通过多阱光学势的设计，研究者成功地实现了等间距的超模式，并且开发了一种二阶离散超对称变换技术，这种技术能够同时激发和检测多个超模式。这种研究不仅克服了分立超模式光子学中的长期瓶颈，还为集成光子通信和智能光计算等新领域的应用奠定了基础。

Method: 本研究的方法包括以下步骤:  首先，研究者设计并构建了一个由精心排列的波导组成的多阱光学势。通过这种多阱结构，超模式可以实现最大的间距，并且具有等间距的效率索引。其次，研究者开发了一种二阶离散超对称变换方法。这种变换方法允许同时激发和检测两个超模式，并且可以通过级联结构扩展到任意数量的超模式。最后，研究者在实验中实现了两个和四个超模式的多复用系统，并验证了方法的有效性和普适性。

Result: 本研究的实验结果证实了提出方法的有效性和普适性。在两个和四个超模式复用系统中，研究者证实了理论预测。所有模式通道在100nm波长范围内（1500-1600纳米）的插入损失均小于2.48dB @1550nm，信道间干扰均小于-18dB @1550nm。在四通道系统中进行的高速光通信实验，实现了1.024Tb/s的数据传输速率并保持了显著低的比特错误率。这表明超模式在集成光子通信中的巨大潜力和高容量。此外，研究者还展示了这些方法在超模式通信技术中的广泛应用潜力。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种系统化的方法来实现分立超模式的等间距分布，并通过高精度激发任意目标超模式。开发的二阶离散超对称变换技术不仅实现了同时激发和检测多个超模式，还可以扩展到任意数量的超模式。实验结果表明，这种方法在集成光子通信和智能光计算等应用中具有广泛的应用潜力。这为集成分立超模式光子学奠定了理论基础，并为未来基于超模式的应用开辟了新的研究方向。

Abstract: We report a systematic methodology to obtain supermodes with equidistant effective index distribution and to excite arbitrary target supermodes with high precision. By employing a multi-well optical potential realized by a judiciously designed waveguide array, the supported supermodes achieve maximal spacing and an equidistant distribution in effective index. More importantly, we develop a 2nd-order discrete supersymmetric (DSUSY) transformation method that enables the excitation and detection of two supermodes at the same time and can be extended to any number of supermodes via simple cascading. Together, these findings overcome the long-standing bottlenecks in integrated supermode photonics and provide an intrinsically scalable route towards harnessing supermodes as a new degree of freedom for encoding, transmitting, and processing information. We experimentally demonstrate the feasibility and universality of this method by realizing two- and four-supermode multiplexing systems. Benefitting from the large effective index spacing between supermodes and the isospectral nature of the DSUSY transformation, the fabricated devices show low insertion losses (< 2.48 dB at 1550 nm) and intermodal crosstalk (< -18 dB at 1550 nm) for all mode channels over a 100-nm wavelength range (1500-1600 nm). The high-speed data transmission experiment performed on the four-channel system achieves an aggregate data rate of 1.024 Tb/s while maintaining considerably low bit error rates, underscoring the potential of supermode photonics for high-capacity on-chip optical communications. This work lays the foundation for integrated supermode photonics, which uses supermodes as a new degree of freedom for light manipulation and opens new avenues for supermode-based applications including but not limited to on-chip optical communications, intelligent optical computing and quantum information technologies.

Abstract: Photonic stepped-frequency (SF) radar offers high range resolution and only requires low-speed driving electronics, but existing architectures face challenges in achieving low phase noise and uniform frequency steps simultaneously. Here, we demonstrate a photonic SF radar system that exploits dual Brillouin lasers in a shared fiber cavity to simultaneously suppress phase noise and ensure uniform frequency stepping. Phase noise is reduced through Brillouin optomechanical suppression and common-mode noise rejection upon photomixing. Frequency-step uniformity is enforced via lasing at a series of uniformly spaced cavity resonances. The system generates an X-band SF waveform spanning 1.31 GHz, achieving >23 dB of phase-noise improvement at a 100 kHz offset relative to a low-cost driving voltage-controlled oscillator. Abstract: We present a numerical study of a divergent-beam Kretschmann surface plasmon resonance (SPR) platform for multiplexed malaria biosensing. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过几何光学极限下的波前分析，假设各向同性介电常数和磁导率，考虑一般3x3的ME矩阵，推导色散关系并分解ME矩阵为迹、对称无迹和反对称部分进行分类研究。

Result: ME矩阵的不同部分对传播效果有不同的影响：迹部分对传播无贡献，反对称部分导致四次色散关系因子分解并产生两种相速度分量，其中包括超前和减慢传播 regimes；对称无迹部分则引入了丰富的方向依赖性，通过不变量影响色散曲面和极化混合。

Abstract: We study electromagnetic wave propagation in homogeneous dielectrics endowed with a linear magnetoelectric (ME) response in the geometric-optics regime. Assuming isotropic permittivity and permeability while keeping a generic $3\times 3$ ME matrix $α_{ij}$, we derive the eikonal (Fresnel) eigenvalue problem for the polarization vector and obtain a compact quartic dispersion relation for the normalized phase speed $r=v/v_d$, where $v_d=(μ\varepsilon)^{-1/2}$ is the phase speed of the underlying dielectric. We then classify the propagation effects of $α_{ij}$ by decomposing it into trace, symmetric-traceless, and antisymmetric sectors. We show that (i) the pure-trace sector is propagation-silent at leading geometric-optics order; (ii) the antisymmetric sector yields a factorized quartic and produces two branches with closed-form phase speeds, including regimes where $|v|>v_d$; and (iii) the symmetric-traceless sector encodes the richest directional dependence through algebraic invariants that control the Fresnel wave surface and polarization mixing. Finally, we discuss how the predicted phase-speed shifts can be accessed by phase-sensitive transmission and resonant techniques, and we outline numerical workflows to validate the analytic dispersion and map polarization signatures in bulk and finite geometries.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 理论分析、数值模拟和实验研究结合。使用多光束交叉配置，计算了不同波长和角度下的光动力学响应并实现了光散射方向的调控。

Result: 通过双光束交叉配置，成功实现了光动力的极大调控，特别是在具有不同波长和角度的光束交叉中实现了逆变、超变或任意转角的光散射能力。多光束交叉配置下，光动力变化幅度很大，并且研究的纳米颗粒具有极高的组分的反射率，表明该系统的响应极其灵敏。

Conclusion: 该研究为开发出基于光散射的纳米粒子排序和高灵敏度光开关提供了理论根据和实验验证。

Abstract: Optical manipulation of Mie-resonant dielectric nanoparticles is strongly influenced by their enhanced scattering and multipolar response, which fundamentally modifiesthe balance of optical forces. In this work, we study the optical forces acting on a resonant dielectric nanoparticle placed near a metal interface, where scattering occurs into both free-space and surface plasmon-polariton (SPP) channels. We show that the interference of electric and magnetic dipole moments leads to highly directional scattering in these channels, and the direction and magnitude of the scattering-induced force are directly linked to the angular directivity of the corresponding radiation channels. We show that in a cross-beam configuration, where the radiation-pressure contribution is suppressed, the optical force can be changed for almost 2π in a wide range of particle sizes that provides a route toward optical sorting of resonant nanoparticles.

</details>


### [156] [Electrically-injected room-temperature waveguide polariton laser](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19513)
*Hassen Souissi,Valentin Develay,Maksym Gromovyi,Edmond Cambril,Christelle Brimont,Laetitia Doyennette,Guillaume Malpuech,Dmitry Solnyshkov,Blandine Alloing,Sebastien Chenot,Mohamed Al-Khalfioui,Eric Frayssinet,Jean-Yves Duboz,Mingyang Zhang,Jesus-Zuniga Perez,Sophie Bouchoule,Thierry Guillet*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: This paper describes room-temperature polariton lasers, achieving mode-locking with 60µm cavities and working even with 20% optical injection. The architecture, similar to ridge-waveguide GaN lasers, uses bulk active region and shows that doped layers for electrical pumping do not hinder polariton lasing. Ex cite more about the specific achievements and implications of the work.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The increasing need for room-temperature laser devices and efficient integration of polariton-based technologies motivate research into new architectures that reduce reliance on optical injection.

Method: The study involves designing, fabricating, and characterizing GaN-based exciton-polariton lasers, with a focus on electrical pumping and mode-locking under different injection levels.

Result: The developed lasers operate without population inversion requirements, demonstrate mode-locking with short cavity lengths, and can function with reduced optical injection. This opens new possibilities for practical polariton device applications without the limitations of traditional setups.

Conclusion: Polariton lasers are viable alternatives to conventional LEDs, especially in areas where device integration is key. The findings pave the way for broader applications of polaritons in optoelectronics by overcoming historical limitations.

Abstract: Exciton-polariton lasers are coherent light sources which do not require the population inversion (transparency) condition to be fulfilled. They have been conceptualized at the end of the XXth century but until now they operate almost exclusively under optical injection, which severely limits the widespread integration of the polariton-based devices implemented so far. Here we tackle this issue by reporting an electrically-pumped exciton-polariton laser based on GaN and operating at room temperature in a mode-locked regime. The laser architecture is close to the geometry of commercial ridge-waveguide GaN lasers, but based on a bulk GaN active region instead of quantum wells. Unique features of polariton lasers are demonstrated, in particular the breakdown of the transparency condition, which enables our polariton lasers to operate even when only a small fraction (20\%) of the cavity length is injected. Moreover, the large polaritonic gain allows for the operation of a short cavity length (60$μm$) compared to commercial lasers. From the very same sample, we also achieve polariton lasing under optical injection, confirming that the doped layers necessary for electrical injection do not prevent strong-coupling nor polariton lasing. Our results open a new perspective for polariton-based devices.

</details>


### [157] [Cross Waveguide Design for Color-Centers in Diamond for Photonic Quantum Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19594)
*Alessio Miranda,Ryoichi Ishihara,Salahuddin Nur*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于交叉型微环结构的 diamond 光栅ectors 器件，适用于量子计算应用中的光子平台，具有高效率、低干扰和紧凑型等特点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着量子计算需求的增加，寻找新型光子平台变得尤为重要。diamond因其优异的光子和自旋性质被广泛研究，但其制备难度较高，限制了在复杂光子电路中的应用。因此，探索 diamond 在光子电路中的可行应用具有重要意义。

Method: 该研究采用设计优化方法，结合交叉型微环结构和辅助支撑结构，实现了高效激发与光子收集，通过减小 crosstalk 和优化工作频段等措施提高了整体性能。同时，注重制造可行性，确保了结构在现代微制造技术下的可行性。

Result: 优化后的结构表现出高效的激发-发射转换率（>5.4%），显著低于 -40 dB 的 crosstalk 描述，工作频段宽达 160 nm，具有良好的制造可行性和机械稳固性。该结构紧凑，脚本面积小于 2000 μm²。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过设计优化，可以实现高性能的 diamond 光栅ectors 器件，为量子计算应用提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Color centers in diamond are a promising platform for quantum computing applications because of their optical and spin properties. However, diamond presents some technological challenges that limit its use in complex or large photonic circuits. To mitigate these limitations, it is technically effective to separate the smallest possible diamond photonic structures or chiplet containing the color center(s) from the rest of the circuit, which is fabricated on another material platform, and then heterogeneously integrate them. Considering efficient excitation and photon collection from waveguide-coupled color centers, we design a cross waveguide as the primary component of our chiplet to access the color centers, channeling excitation and emitted photons into different waveguides, and connecting the structure to the other components of the photonic circuit. The chiplet containing the cross waveguide and supporting structures requires careful optimization of each subcomponent. The receptor's design is also critical for optimal signal transmission. In this paper, we develop a simple but efficient methodology to optimize the main components constituting both the chiplet and the receptor for their synergistic operation. The designed structure has an excitation-to-emission conversion of more than 5.4%, crosstalk of less than -40 dB, a working bandwidth of 160 nm, fabrication feasibility and tolerance within the limits of modern nanofabrication, and a mechanical solid structure with a footprint of less than 2000 $μ$m

</details>
